Songjiang 65

The Command Executed Eight Bandit Criminals by Shooting: The chief of the fourth district of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Team, who previously arrested six pirates in the Wusong area, Zhang Shangxian, Qu Jiakai, Chen Dakao, Chen Xianjuan, You Zhaoyun, and You Zhaomeng, and Fan Guozhong, the leader of the first team of the first district, who arrested two members of the Taibao A Shu gang, Wei Hongxiang and Gan Azuo, in Shanghai, confessed to the robberies and other cases under interrogation by the Songhu Pacification Division Command. They were sentenced to death in accordance with the provisions of the Punishment of Bandits Ordinance. Today (29th), Commander Cao followed the order, signed and extracted the six pirates Zhang Shangxian, etc., and the two criminals Wei Hongxiang, etc., verified their identities, announced their crimes, and ordered them to be bound to the execution ground and executed by shooting.

The Power of Bandits in the Ninth District Is Gradually Increasing: In Xiaokunshan Township, which belongs to the county, there have been several cases of small gangs of bandits committing robberies and kidnappings with weapons in groups of six or seven. The police force of the public security police station in the district is weak and difficult to protect. Wang Huankun, the director of the Ninth District, has personally requested the county public security bureau to allocate weapons and ammunition to strengthen its strength. It is reported that last night, a certain family not far from the town was threatened by bandits to extort money, demanding 1,400 yuan. They first took 400 yuan, and the remaining amount was allowed to be delivered at Meijialong at a later date. The cunning of the bandits is evident.

Suzhou 66

The Cui Qingshan Appeal Case Is Scheduled for Sentencing: The former Suqian County Magistrate Cui Qingshan was initially sentenced to two years in prison and fined 1,000 yuan for dereliction of duty and fraud. Cui refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the High Court, which held a hearing yesterday, announced the end of the debate, and scheduled sentencing for December 3.

Expediting the Payment of Arrears for Education Funds: The education funds for various primary schools in Wuxian County have been in arrears for three months. Representatives of various schools have repeatedly urged the Education Bureau to pay them, but to no avail. Yesterday, representatives of the school principals again urged the Education Bureau to pay them. Director Wu promised to raise funds for one and a half months on Tuesday. The principals' meeting also decided on that day that if the funds are still not released on Tuesday, the schools will not be able to maintain themselves and can only convene a general meeting to discuss countermeasures.

Wuxi 67

Director of the Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau Accused of Dismissal: Yu Xilin, the director of the local tobacco and alcohol monopoly bureau, has been harshly exploiting merchants since taking office, causing them to suffer. Recently, Yang Lubing, the chairman of the soy sauce industry association, listed the evidence and filed a complaint with the province. The Ministry of Finance's stamp tobacco and alcohol tax bureau and the Jiangsu stamp tobacco and alcohol tax bureau successively dispatched representatives to Wuxi to conduct thorough investigations of the chamber of commerce and liquor merchants. There is considerable evidence, and it is reported that Director Yu has been dismissed by the provincial government.

Please Cancel the Electricity Deposit: The Qishuyan Power Plant recently sent letters to various users, asking them to pay an electricity deposit. Wang Kuihe and 178 other users in the Beiqu Daqiao Town responded after receiving the letter that the users pay electricity bills monthly according to the current used. If there is any late payment, the factory will definitely order the craftsmen to cut off the electricity, which is already a thorough prevention. There is absolutely no need for a deposit. They specifically sent a letter to the Daqiao Town Office to forward it to the Qishuyan Power Plant, asking them to withdraw the order. Town Chief Miao Lianchen forwarded the letter to the plant yesterday, asking them to withdraw the order immediately. However, other users in the urban area have also jointly made a request to withdraw the order, and will not stop until they achieve their goal.

Zhenjiang 68

County Magistrates of Five Counties Come to the Province for Official Business: Zhang Pengzhu, the county magistrate of Wujin County, Li Qinming, the county magistrate of Siyang County, Wang Guanxian, the county magistrate of Gaochun County, Wang Jiwu, the county magistrate of Danyang County, and Shen Yong, the county magistrate of Songjiang County, all came to the province yesterday for official business. They plan to meet with Director Hu of the Civil Affairs Department today to personally report everything.

Zhenjiang 69

The Gaoyou breach plugging is complete. The two major breaches at Junlou and Miaoxiangkou in Gaoyou, one 160 zhang long and the other 90 zhang long, were not far apart and were the most difficult breaches to plug in the canal embankment. This time, Director Shen of the Construction Bureau selected and appointed Yu Heng as the director of the breach plugging project. Yu first built a levee on the west bank and then built dams upstream and downstream of the two breaches to cut off the flow. Construction began on October 12th, and by the 24th of this month, the northern section of the west levee and the upstream and downstream dams had been joined. As for the southern section of the west levee, because the opening was narrowed, the water level rose more than a zhang, forming a waterfall, making construction extremely difficult. Yu supervised the workers and worked hard, and finally, on the 26th of this month, the breach was safely joined in a storm. Once the earth levee is completed, the flow can be cut off. The entire project for Junlou and Miaoxiang has been successfully completed.

Nantong 70

The Dada Steamer was Robbed at Liuxu The Shanghai-Yangzhou route's Dada Company's Dada steamer set sail upstream from Tianshenggang, Nantong on the 27th. At about 1:00 AM on the 28th, while passing the Liuxu river area under the jurisdiction of Taixing County, it was suddenly robbed by bandits, resulting in heavy losses. Fortunately, no one was injured. After being robbed, the steamer sailed to the port and telegraphed a report to Shanghai. It arrived in Yangzhou at dawn on the 28th.

Three Kidnappers Executed Liang's Troops Stationed in Tong seized kidnappers Qin Mingfu, Li Futai, Yan Chenxian, etc., and recovered a large number of firearms while patrolling the Zhangzhishan area along the river. They also rescued eight Jiangnan hostages, men and women. The captured bandits confessed to the crime. Commander Pan telegraphed Chief Commander Liang for instructions. On the 28th, he received an order to escort the three bandits to Zhangzhishan Town for execution.

Yangzhou 71

Director Shen Inspects the Laisheng'an Section of the River Project Shao Fuchen, Director of the Public Works Department of Jiangdu, because Construction Director Shen will inspect the project at Laisheng'an, specially dispatched a ferry early on the 27th to welcome him. It is reported that Shen went directly to the worksite and did not disembark in Yangzhou. The proposed construction plan for river-blocking dams has been decided to be built at the Yukou and Tonghu sluice gates. Surveyors have been sent to measure the shallow滩 in the outer lake to facilitate the use of dredging boats to dredge the channel to a depth sufficient for small轮 to navigate, so that small轮 on the Tongyang postal route can detour through the outer lake. After dredging, construction will begin to cut off the flow and facilitate the plugging of the Laisheng'an breach.

Educational News

Special Feature 72

Anti-Japanese National Salvation's Vital Force (Asia) 73

More than seventy days after the successive fall of various parts of the Northeast, it was only then that the professors of various universities in Shanghai, who hold the leading position in national knowledge, formed an anti-Japanese national salvation organization. One cannot help but sigh at how the nation is in such dire straits, how could they endure so long. However, at this critical moment when the strength and voices of the national masses are about to run out, this unique vital force stands out. In addition to feeling extremely excited, we extend our infinite hopes.

First, given the state of the country, neither war nor peace is feasible, and indecision is even less feasible. However, if everyone is truly determined to die for the country, then war is a solution. If one has the ability to endure the pain for a while, then peace is also a solution. Alas, in today's country, there are only a few: (1) traitors who seek personal gain at the expense of the country, (2) warmongers driven by momentary emotions, (3) those who are ignorant and follow the emperor's orders, and (4) incompetent meat-eaters who are at a loss. Alas, with such national difficulties, such people, and such a government, the future of the Chinese nation is fraught with unprecedented dangers. Professors are all scholars with deep learning and reflection. The association has clearly stipulated that "research" is one of the important tasks of its members. It is hoped that they will systematically and comprehensively study the issue and arrive at a factual conclusion regarding war and peace, and then use various methods to urgently achieve practical results. This is the most crucial issue among the current difficult problems, and it urgently awaits a calm, rational answer, or even more effective emotional stimulation. Since the meat-eaters have failed to plan for the long term, it is hoped that those who call themselves professors will take on this responsibility. We further hope to assess the true value of today's university education from this.

Second, professors usually have their own specialties and are less involved in association affairs. However, their legitimate personal rights should not be abandoned. I believe that in the future, there will definitely be those who consider giving up the right to vote as a crime. And in the current national crisis, the civic duty brooks no exception. The purpose of the association must lie in this. Although there are many methods of resisting Japan and saving the country, merely relying on theory is ineffective. Since the general public's level of education is so low, even realistic, objective arguments, such as statistics and comparisons, may have little effect. We sincerely hope that all professors will use their expertise, not only to think but also to take action, to perform brave and effective deeds.

Third, even if you gather all the world's most skilled architects, you cannot build a mansion. It requires the hard work of countless laborers. The professors should not be too arrogant and just discuss plans on paper, forgetting the masses of people who possess great power and are anxious and unable to live in peace. We firmly believe that only by leading the vast army of the people can we resist Japan and save the country. This depends on the association's propositions and methods.

In conclusion, concerning the anti-Japanese national salvation association of the so-called professor class, amidst extreme grief and hardship, we cannot help but hope that the association will make unique contributions. Why is the 5,000-year-old Chinese nation so weak today? May the Shanghai universities' anti-Japanese national salvation association, rising as an unexpected force, catch up quickly.

Local News

Shanghai Universities 74

Professors Establish Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association

In view of the escalating national crisis, professors from various universities in Shanghai held a meeting at the Xinxin Hotel at 12:00 noon yesterday (the 29th) to exchange views. More than 100 people attended the meeting. As a result, they passed a resolution to organize the Shanghai Universities' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association and elected Xie Xunchu, Jin Tongyin, Wang Zaoqiu, Wu Zelin, and Yu Nanqiu as directors, and Shen Junru, Lu Dingkui, Huang Zhongsu, Zheng Tonghe, and Chen Xuanxian as alternate directors. They immediately sent a telegram to the government, opposing the designation of Jinzhou as a neutral zone. The telegram read as follows: "The Northeast is our territory, and Jinzhou is the seat of our Liaoning Provincial Government. Designating it as a neutral zone is tantamount to abandoning our sovereignty. Therefore, we telegraph to you, requesting that Representative Shi immediately withdraw this proposal and continue to insist on Japan's troop withdrawal as a prerequisite. We also order the Northeast troops to strictly defend their positions and not to withdraw to the interior, so as to protect our territory. We eagerly await your response." As for the general assembly's declaration, the principles have already been passed on the spot. The full text will be published soon.

Nanjing-Bound University 75

Petition Delegation Returns to Shanghai Yesterday

Petition Delegation Holds Closing Meeting

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of Students from various universities in this city sent a delegation of more than 5,000 people to Nanjing to urge the government to send troops. As a result of the petition, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek responded to the four points raised one by one. The petition delegation was satisfied and returned to Shanghai yesterday. The following is a report from a Shanghai News Agency reporter on the situation of the delegation's return to Shanghai. The first group of more than 2,000 people arrived in Shanghai at 12:00 noon yesterday. The second group arrived in Shanghai at 1:30 PM on the same day. Representatives of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association and various schools gathered at the North Railway Station to welcome them, along with representatives from the militia and other organizations, numbering approximately 3,000 people. The sound of military music and firecrackers was incessant, and the scene was majestic. The commander-in-chief of the welcoming group was Yuan Yiqun from Jiaotong University, and the chief disciplinarian was Nie Haifan from Zhonggong. After the delegation arrived at the station, they all removed their hats to pay their respects and shouted slogans: (1) Welcome the delegation to Nanjing to urge the government to send troops back to Shanghai! (2) Down with Japanese imperialism! (3) Long live the mass movement! (4) Long live the Republic of China! After shouting the slogans, they were escorted back to their respective schools. It is also reported that the delegation of students from various universities in Shanghai who went to Nanjing to urge the government to send troops held its last meeting in Nanjing at 9:00 AM yesterday. The meeting was chaired by Zhou Xiaobo from Fudan University and recorded by Soochow University. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Regarding the case of how to deal with the fact that the principals of various schools in Shanghai, under the orders of the government's standing committee, published notices to stop students' patriotic movement, it was resolved to submit a warning to the student union in the name of the delegation to Nanjing to urge the government to send troops. (2) Regarding how to report the expenses of the Nanjing trip, it was resolved that the general affairs department of the delegation would report it orally. (3) Regarding how the accounts should be audited, it was resolved that Jinan, Zhizhi, and Datong Universities would jointly be responsible for the audit. (4) Regarding the case of the Shanghai newspapers' clarification of the rumors about the delegation's school site, it was resolved that the secretariat would handle it as appropriate. (5) Regarding the case of ending the delegation and handing it over, it was resolved that Fudan University would jointly handle the handover with the general affairs department and the secretariat. (6) Regarding the case of when and where to hold the delegation's closing meeting, it was resolved that the date would be set for this Friday (December 4th) at 2:00 PM at the New Youth Association near the Great World.

It is also reported that the delegation received extensive assistance from all sectors of the capital during this trip to Nanjing. In addition to issuing declarations and reporting everything, they expressed their sincere gratitude to all sectors of the local community. In addition, it is reported that the details of the delegation's trip to Nanjing to urge the government to send troops will be compiled and published by Shanghai News Agency reporters Guan Zhaozheng, Pan Chuji, and Yang Shuchang in the coming days.

(8) The case of the Youth Volunteer Rescue Team going to Heilongjiang within a limited time was resolved to be handled by the Military Affairs Committee. (9) The case of determining the date of the general review of the Youth Volunteer Army was resolved to be before December 10th. (10) The case of Guanghua holding a second local district propaganda campaign was rejected. (11) The case of Guanghua proposing a second propaganda campaign in other cities was rejected. (12) The case of Daxia proposing a costume parade was approved and handed over to the Propaganda Department of the Executive Committee for handling. (13) The case of requesting the Municipal Party Department to subsidize the costume parade with 500 yuan was approved. (14) The case of recommending that student anti-Japanese national salvation associations in various provinces and cities guide student anti-Japanese national salvation associations in various places was approved. (15) The case of various schools organizing research committees on Sino-Japanese issues was approved. (16) The case of Daxia proposing that the people of the whole country generally do not recognize any explicit or secret treaties signed with foreign countries by either the Nanjing or Guangdong government before a unified government is produced after September 18th was not discussed. (17) The case of three apprentice Qian Caian and others from the Xishang Labor Bureau being detained and expelled for informing on shopkeepers who privately sold Japanese goods and requesting assistance from the association was resolved to publish news to expose the truth and request the Municipal Party Department to help maintain their jobs.

Announcement by the Municipal Education Bureau and Public Security Bureau 77

Stop Middle School Students from Raising National Salvation Funds

The Education Bureau held a meeting at 2:00 PM on the 30th of this month

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau and Public Security Bureau issued an announcement to stop middle school students from donating to national salvation funds. It stated, "It is important for middle and primary school students in this city to go out to raise national salvation funds. It is commendable that students are patriotic and enthusiastically advocating donations. However, this is not a local matter and should be carried out jointly after a concrete plan is made. Repeated donations by students can easily lose social sympathy. Before proper measures are established, donations should be stopped immediately. In addition to separate orders, this announcement is hereby issued for compliance. November 28th, 20th year of the Republic of China. Director Xu Peihuang, Director Chen Xizeng." Furthermore, the Shanghai Education Bureau issued announcement Shang Zi No. 8 regarding the disposal of already raised national salvation funds. It stated, "The donation of funds for national salvation by middle and primary school students has been jointly announced with the Public Security Bureau to be stopped immediately. All funds already raised by various schools shall be gathered at this bureau at 2:00 PM on the 30th of this month, with each school sending one staff member and two students, carrying the donation bamboo tubes. The Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of Middle School Students shall send one standing committee member to gather at this bureau, and the Municipal Government shall be requested to send personnel to jointly supervise the opening of the tubes and deposit the funds into the bank for compliance. This announcement, November 28th, 20th year of the Republic of China, Director Xu Peihuang."

Meeting of Representatives of Middle School Student Petitioners 78

Executive Committee and Economic Committee Meetings Also Held

The petition delegation of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of Middle School Students in this city arrived in Shanghai at 4:00 AM the day before yesterday (28th) (a small number of students had already arrived in Shanghai on the afternoon of the 27th). The delegation held the sixth delegation meeting at Minli Middle School on Zhonghua Road at 2:00 PM yesterday, with more than 20 schools participating, including Shanghai Middle School, Pudong, Zhengfeng, and Xinmin. The presidium consisted of Zhao Fu from Shanghai University, Li Bin from Huinan, Chen Yubai from Wuben, and Zhou Jialiang from Shanghai Middle School. Liu Tongbao from Chizhong served as the recorder. After performing the formalities, the discussion began immediately after the chairman's report.

Matters for Discussion: (1) How should the petition process be reported to the Student Union? It was resolved that the presidium would be responsible for drafting a report and submitting it. (2) When should the remaining funds of the delegation be returned? It was resolved that the general affairs department would settle the accounts within one week for return. (3) It was resolved to request the Student Union to send letters of appreciation to the various organizations that hosted the petition delegation. (4) It was resolved to request the Student Union to punish the representatives of the delegation who were derelict in their duties. (5) It was resolved to send letters to various newspapers and the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Station in the name of the delegation, stating that middle school students did not destroy the station. (6) Should a letter to fellow citizens be published regarding the petition? It was resolved to publish it in the name of the "Shanghai Middle School Students Delegation to Nanjing to Petition". (7) How should the delegation hand over to the Student Union? It was resolved that the presidium would handle it jointly with the heads of the various departments. (8) The news report on the 28th stated that more than 500 middle school petition students returned to Shanghai on the 26th. After investigation, it was found to be inconsistent with the facts and a letter should be sent for correction. It was resolved to approve the adjournment after the discussion. After the delegation meeting, the 16th meeting was continued.

Executive Committee Meeting The representatives attending the Executive Committee meeting were Zhao Lianfu, Chairman of Shanghai Middle School, Minli Girls' High School, Chengzhong, Jingye, Minli, Wuben, Xinmin, Soochow No. 2 Middle School, Qingxin, Shanghai University Affiliated High School, and Pudong. Yu Zhongbiao, representative of the Municipal Party Department, was present as a nonvoting member. "Matters Resolved": (1) How should assistance be provided to the Public Middle School's Dean of Students who opened the donation bamboo tube and left the school with the money? It was resolved that the inspection division would investigate first and then discuss the measures. (2) All schools should stop raising national salvation funds externally at 6:00 PM on the 30th, and internal donations within the school should still be stopped on December 6th. The resolution was approved. (3) The donation tubes from all schools should be collected on December 1st and a public tube-breaking ceremony should be held. It was resolved to send a notice inviting the Municipal Party Department and principals of various middle schools to jointly monitor the ceremony with two representatives. (4) The general review of the student volunteer army of all middle schools on December 1st should be postponed because they have just returned from Nanjing and the preparations are insufficient. It was resolved to approve the postponement to December 7th.

Economic Committee Meeting The meeting was held at Minli Middle School on Zhonghua Road at 2:00 PM yesterday. The chairman was Hui Ling Li Bin, and the recorder was Han Xuezhang from Minzhi. After performing the formalities, the discussion began. "Matters for Discussion" (1) The committee should have one chairman and one secretary. It was resolved to approve it. (2) Stipulate the date of the committee meeting. It was resolved that regular meetings would be held once every two weeks, and special meetings would be convened by the chairman. (3) Elect committee staff. It was resolved that Hui Ling would be the chairman and the Minzhi Girls' School would be the secretary. (4) Stipulate the committee's office hours. It was resolved that each school would have one day of office hours per week, and it would be distributed as follows: Monday, Yuqing Middle School; Tuesday, Shanghai Girls' High School; Wednesday, Minzhi Girls' School; Thursday, Zhengfeng; Friday, Qingxin Girls' School; Saturday, Hui Ling; Sunday, Qixiu Girls' School. (5) How to resolve the Student Union's current economic panic? It was resolved that: (A) Request the Anti-Japanese Association of various sectors in this city to subsidize the association's regular expenses with 200 yuan per month. (B) Request the Municipal Party Department to increase the association's subsidy by 100 yuan per month. (C) Committee members must assist the affairs department of the Executive Committee in collecting regular fees from various schools within the next week. (6) Stipulate the fee collection area for each committee member. It was resolved that the chairman would stipulate it.

Hu Hanmin Telegraphed Shanghai Yesterday 94

The Guangdong Dispute Resolved

The Fourth Plenary Session Will Continue

Delegates Who Had Withdrawn Are Returning to the Province One After Another

Hu Hanmin, Sun Ke, and Wu Chaoshu all arrived in Guangzhou from Hong Kong last night and, upon arrival, immediately telegraphed Shanghai, saying that the Fourth Plenary Session of Guangdong had accepted the mediation of Hu and Wu and would continue the session immediately, accommodating the resolutions of the Shanghai Peace Conference and proceeding with the election of the Fourth Central Executive and Supervisory Committee members in accordance with the methods determined by the peace conference. The telegram also stated that Hu, Wu, and Sun all took a ship to Guangzhou last night, and the delegates who had withdrawn were also returning to the province one after another to attend the Fourth Plenary Session. The prospects for peace are extremely optimistic.

July 31st This Year 95

The French Court's Judgment is Invalid

Because the Agreement Explicitly Stipulates that it Takes Effect from July 31st

Whether the judgment made by the Shanghai French Concession Mixed Court on July 31st this year is valid, as presented by the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court to the Judicial Department, was referred to the Judicial Yuan. Yesterday, the Judicial Yuan instructed that since the agreement to establish a Chinese court in the Shanghai French Concession explicitly stipulates that it takes effect from July 31st this year, the judgment made by the former Mixed Court on July 31st this year is naturally invalid, and the case should still be adjudicated by the court in accordance with the law.

The Fuzhou-Bound New Ming 97

Will Sail Today at Noon

Will Stop at the Otaru Wharf in Japan

Requesting the American Merchant to Handle the Pilot

Changing Berth to the American Merchant Wharf The China Merchants Bureau received an order from the Ministry of Communications to dispatch the Beiyang steamship "New Ming" to Japan to transport overseas Chinese back to their country. The "New Ming" foreign passenger ship's licenses and other documents have been prepared by the Ministry of Communications in consultation with the Customs. The most important matters are the pilot for going to Japan and the wharf to dock at in Yokohama. The Bureau has consulted with the American merchant Otaru Company in this port. When the "New Ming" arrives in Japan, Otaru will be asked to hire a pilot on its behalf. When the ship arrives in Yokohama, it will berth at the Otaru Wharf so that overseas Chinese can board the ship. After days of consultation, it is said that Otaru has agreed and has telegraphed its Yokohama branch to prepare.

Preparing a Large Amount of Food Supplies The problems of the pilot and wharf for the "New Ming" to Japan have been resolved, and there are no other difficulties. Because there are a total of 1,200 to 1,300 overseas Chinese returning to the country this time, the demand for food on the ship will be huge. It must be purchased in Shanghai first. It is estimated that at least six days' worth of food must be prepared for these thousand-plus people after they board the ship. Yesterday, the Bureau allocated funds and handed them over to the "New Ming" shipowner, instructing the stewards to purchase everything in Shanghai and store it on the ship.

Setting Sail East Today at Noon The cargo brought by the "New Ming" from Tianjin this time has been unloaded. The ship will sail to Japan empty and needs ballast. Yesterday, the shipping department ordered the ship to prepare this and load enough coal for fourteen days. It is approved to set sail east at noon today, heading directly from Shanghai to Yokohama. The journey is expected to take about five days.

Telegraphing to Inform the Consulate The date of departure for the "New Ming" to Japan to transport overseas Chinese has been telegraphed by the China Merchants Bureau to the Ministry of Communications, requesting that it be forwarded to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, ordering our Consul-General in Yokohama to take care of the "New Ming" upon its arrival and to liaise with the Japanese Customs authorities on all matters. Overseas Chinese who should take the ship back to the country are also ordered to gather in Yokohama so that they can board the ship after it arrives, in order to avoid delaying the schedule. The Bureau has also telegraphed Consul Zhou in Yokohama directly.

Song Yuanyuan 99

Talks About Saving the Country Through Aviation

Fujian Province Has Already Donated Over 2.9 Million

Planning to Promote it Nationwide in Shanghai

He Jingzhi Intends to Establish a Factory Jointly Funded by China and the United States

According to the Huadong News Agency, Fujian Province has recently launched an aviation-based national salvation movement and has already received donations of 2.98 million. Currently, it is still actively in progress. Yesterday, the executive committee member Song Yuanyuan came to Shanghai to purchase aircraft and plans to promote the movement nationwide to strengthen national defense. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency specially visited Mr. Song at his private residence yesterday, and he talked about various matters as follows:

The Origin of the Initiative According to Mr. Song, he has been away from Fujian for more than four years. Recently, he returned and passed through Xiamen, where various community organizations came to visit him, because the foreign insult is imminent, and Xiamen is especially noticed by the Japanese. They asked him to discuss with the community organizations in Zhangzhou and Commander Zhang Zhen to convene representatives from various counties in southern Fujian in Zhangzhou to jointly discuss national salvation and self-defense strategies. After Mr. Song arrived in Zhangzhou, he immediately discussed with all sectors and believed that the issue of saving the country should not be empty talk but should be studied on the basis of facts, especially on the basis of military preparedness. Our country has more than two million regular troops, making it the world's leading army country. However, the quality of soldiers is more important than quantity. Moreover, the combat effectiveness of this conscripted army is even more limited. Recently, people from all walks of life have advocated changing to a conscription system, and the voices are quite high. It is expected that it can be realized soon. However, the effect of implementing conscription will be seen several years later, which is not enough to be a current strategy to resist foreign insults. Secondly, research on the navy shows that our country's navy suffered a setback in the Sino-Japanese War. Although the naval authorities proposed a plan to revive the navy the year before last, it was shelved due to financial difficulties. However, even if this plan is implemented, its effect will be seen in twenty or thirty years, which is not enough to be a current strategy to resist foreign insults. When I was serving in Nanjing, I talked with various central committee members about our country's military preparedness and had research on the two issues of submarines and aviation. I said that the manufacturing of submarines is considered a secret technology by various countries, and it is not easy to get its transmission. If we buy from various countries, they will definitely not let us have the excellent ones. If we want something easy and quick to achieve and cost-effective, we should follow the aviation-based national salvation legacy of the Prime Minister first. Many committee members agreed. In recent years, the government has paid great attention to the aviation industry, but the progress is still slow due to the current financial difficulties. People in Fujian want to seek national salvation and self-defense in practice and should first promote civilian-run aviation as a backing for the government. All sectors agreed, and Commander Zhang also strongly supported it. Therefore, Mr. Lin Zhiren and others were publicly elected to send a telegram to initiate the Fujian Aviation National Salvation Association.

The Progress of the Situation Mr. Lin and others initiated the Fujian Aviation Association, thinking that the overall situation was critical and the traffic in northern Fujian was blocked, making it difficult to convene. Therefore, they asked various counties in southern Fujian to first send representatives to meet in Zhangzhou on the 8th of this month. On that day, representatives from more than 20 counties attended the meeting. Chen Guohui, the Brigade Commander of Quanzhou, sent representative Ye Zuyi, Lin Guogeng, the Naval Commander of Xiamen, sent representative Zhao Zhixiong, and Commander Zhang also attended. They immediately announced the establishment of the Fujian Aviation National Salvation Association to preside over the civilian-run aviation affairs of the entire province. After passing the articles of association, they also agreed that each county and overseas Chinese port should make donations. The aircraft purchased should be named after the county or port, and those purchased by individuals should be named after them. The aircraft should be formed into teams, which would be used for transportation in peacetime and assist the national army in attack and defense in times of resistance or suppression of the Communists. In addition, because there was a shortage of aviation talents in Fujian Province, it was decided to establish aviation schools in a short period of time to recruit students from various counties and ports to train specialized talents in driving and manufacturing. At the continued meeting on the 9th, in addition to electing executive and supervisory committee members and custodians, the representatives of each county jointly discussed the amount of donations, which should be proportional to wealth. Siming County recognized 500,000 as the most, followed by Longxi and Jinjiang, each with 200,000, and Dehua and Yongtai each with 20,000 as the least. All officers and soldiers of Zhang Zhen's department donated one month's salary and recognized 300,000, and Chen Guohui's brigade also recognized a donation of 150,000. Because the representatives of Putian, Xianyou, and other counties had not arrived, the conference also compared and tentatively decided that a total of 2.98 million had been recognized for donation. Commander Zhang and the representatives of various counties also agreed to first pay 600,000 within two weeks, which would be kept by Committee Member Huang Yizhu and others for the purpose of ordering aircraft. At the same time, they telegraphed the provincial government and various counties that had not recognized donations to uniformly initiate the movement and telegraphed various overseas Chinese ports to collect large sums of money, and it is expected that the effect will not be small.

Coming to Shanghai to Purchase Aircraft and also, in order to purchase aircraft, they should first apply to the Aviation Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs for a passport. The Fujian Aviation Association initially elected Commander Zhang to go to Beijing to get the passport and elected me to come to Shanghai to contact leaders from all walks of life to promote the movement nationwide. Later, Commander Zhang received a telegram from Beijing saying that defense was important and asked him to postpone his trip. Therefore, the aviation association entrusted me to handle matters related to obtaining the passport and purchasing the aircraft.

Planning to Set Up a Factory to Manufacture Themselves Currently, Minister He Jingzhi is in Shanghai to discuss the aviation-based national salvation movement in Fujian Province. Mr. He expressed his sympathy and suggested that it would be too uneconomical to purchase from foreign countries. Currently, there are foreign merchants planning to establish an aircraft manufacturing plant jointly funded with our country, with a capital of about 10 million. If a portion of the funds in Fujian Province can be retained as share capital, it will be even more beneficial. This idea is very good. If more than ten provinces have successfully established civilian-run aviation, tens of millions of funds can be raised, and one or two tenths can be used to set up a factory to manufacture themselves. Once the negotiations are completed in Shanghai, they will go to Beijing again to discuss everything with Mr. He.

Contacts in Shanghai Mr. Song also said that the national salvation movement in Shanghai's various community organizations is very enthusiastic, and there are also many who advocate civilian-run aviation. I originally intended to immediately convene leaders of various community organizations to discuss and initiate the Aviation National Salvation Association. However, before the initiation, there must be a backbone person responsible for formulating the steps to be taken so that it can be easily effective. Moreover, Shanghai is the center of national public opinion and economy and has a great influence on politics. This national salvation undertaking is related to the security and survival of the country. If the research and preparation are not mature in advance, the effect may be very small in the future and may even create obstacles. Therefore, I am now exchanging opinions with various parties and asking various leaders to come forward to preside over the movement. It is expected that a method will be formulated within a few days and then the movement can begin. I plan to wait for the establishment of the civilian aviation organization and notify various provinces and cities, and then go to Ningbo to handle the passport, purchase aircraft, and discuss setting up a factory to manufacture aircraft. Now I hope that various newspapers will strongly promote the movement. If various provinces and cities uniformly initiate the movement, thousands of civilian-run aircraft can be added within a few months. Using this as a backing for the government will have real strength. In terms of the current resistance against foreign insults, Japan is an island country, and its invading troops must be protected by the navy. Warships are most afraid of aircraft. If we first drive away their navy, their landing troops will be cut off from the rear supply and will inevitably be disarmed by us. Therefore, in planning a strategy to resist foreign insults, I dare say that saving the country must promote aviation, and aviation can definitely save the country.

Articles of Association of the Aviation Association (1) This association follows Mr. Sun Yat-sen's aviation-based national salvation legacy and gathers the strength of the people of the entire province and overseas Chinese to run aviation undertakings, named the Fujian Aviation National Salvation Association. (2) This association takes civilian-run aviation power as a backing for the government's suppression of the Communists and resistance against foreign insults and is subject to the command and supervision of the central aviation supreme authority and the local military authorities to carry out all matters that should be handled, but not for any internal strife. (3) The association's headquarters will be temporarily located in Zhangzhou. (4) This association is organized by representatives of various counties and ports that have joined (holding a representative conference). Members of the branch associations in various counties and ports are all members of this association. (5) This association elects executive and supervisory committee members by the representative conference to organize two committees, and then the executive and supervisory committees mutually elect standing committee members to manage all affairs of the association. (6) This association has an attached planning committee, which is composed of experts hired by the executive committee and is subject to the command and supervision of the executive committee to handle all plans. (7) The executive committee has general affairs, navigation, and publicity sections, each with one director and many staff members, who are appointed and dismissed by the standing committee and direct the various sections to handle affairs. (8) This association designates banks in various counties and ports to collect funds, which are responsible for safekeeping by the estimated safekeeping committee. (9) The association's expenses, in addition to the subsidy from the military and political officers, are borne separately by the branch associations in various counties and ports. (10) These articles of association are decided and passed by the representative conference and request that the local military authorities forward them to the central aviation authority for approval and record.

Explaining the Meaning of the Execution of the Agreement 101

Referring to All Litigation Documents and Judgments

The Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court submitted a request to the Judicial and Administrative Department to verify the meaning of execution mentioned in Article 5 of the agreement on the establishment of a Chinese court in the Shanghai Concession. The Judicial and Administrative Department forwarded it to the Judicial Yuan. Yesterday, the Judicial Yuan instructed that the execution mentioned in Article 5 of the agreement refers to all litigation documents and judgments. As for the disposition of confiscated items after execution, it should still be handled in accordance with Article 493 of the Criminal Procedure Law.

He Xiangning's Talk After Arriving in Shanghai 102

Handling First Aid for Japanese Soldiers with National Qualifications

Japan and France Want to Join Hands to Dominate The Chinese People Should Save Themselves Quickly

Yu Youren Came to Shanghai from Beijing and Invited He to Go to Beijing Together

Madam He Xiangning, the wife of Liao Zhongkai, arrived in Shanghai from France on the French mail ship "Maishanqi" the day before yesterday and is staying at Madam Sun Yat-sen's residence on Molly Avenue. A reporter from the Xinzhen News Agency visited her upon her arrival, but she was out. Yesterday, Madam He moved to Gan Naiguang's place for a temporary stay, and the reporter visited her again in the evening and was granted an audience. The conversation was as follows: Madam Liao said that she left Shanghai for Europe in September the year before last and stayed abroad for a total of two years and two months, mostly in France, and also went to England and Germany for a period of time. In ordinary times, she lived in Europe, and in addition to painting and reading for entertainment, she operated her own clothing, food, and other items. This time, because of the pain of the national disaster, she will handle first aid and other matters for Japanese wounded soldiers with national qualifications. She does not intend to participate in domestic politics in nineteen cases. Therefore, when I passed through Hong Kong, I did not go to Guangzhou, only to Shantou, because my (He called herself) mother was buried there, and I went to see her tomb. This time, among the European countries, apart from England and the United States being closer to us, France's attitude towards us is the worst. France

Page 10

has clearly shown that it wants Japan to join hands and the two countries to dominate East Asia. When this matter happened not long ago, our country planned to invite the press in Paris to report the truth, but it was not possible. The Parisian press completely followed the Japanese. Therefore, it is not advisable for our country to rely on the League of Nations to resolve the matter. The League of Nations is actually a group in which major countries carve up small countries and divide up honesty. We have no other strategy but to save ourselves daily. Now that I have arrived in Shanghai, I plan to hold a calligraphy and painting exhibition within a week or ten days, and then I will reside in Shanghai and engage in the first aid work of the Red Cross Society.

Yu and Others Invite He to Go to Beijing Yu Youren, the President of the Supervisory Yuan of the National Government, arrived in Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai express train at about 8 AM yesterday. At about 5 PM yesterday, he and Zhou Qigang and Ding Chaowu, members of the Central Committee, visited her one after another. In addition to talking with Madam He about the internal and external situation, Yu and others invited Madam He to go to Beijing. Madam He expressed that she was unwell and would not go anywhere else for the time being.

Madam Liao's Recent Poems Madam He also showed her recent works and attached a short introduction, saying, "The Japanese disaster has befallen the motherland. Passing through Annam, I was moved by the sound of the song. One poem written in the boat in November of the 20th year: I am afraid to hear the sound of singing the national ruin, and I want to stop and chant because of the heartbreak. There is a way to revive the country, the virtue of Emperor Wen, weeping for the sin of stopping the car, Xia Yu Ren, losing all the allies, who can love and comfort the common people? Every common man has a duty to rise and fall. The people under the spring should be full of tears. I am afraid to hear the sound of singing the national ruin, wandering on the road, and doubling my sadness. What is the weight of sacrificing rights? Where to find the lost rivers and mountains? The leaves fall in the Xiao Xiao, and the wild geese fly south, wandering thousands of miles back to the motherland. The events before and after the eight years in the Central Plains teach people to recall tears on their clothes. Three years of facing the wall like Vimalakirti, the right and wrong are unclear. The unbaked soil is not dry, and the strong neighbor does not destroy itself. I have been wandering in Paris for three years, dreaming of Liaoning and Ning, and the lungs are fried. Such a Jiangshan is fragmented, and the slave insults without words."

Ten-Man Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps 103

Yesterday Held General Meeting of Members

Swore Oath to Prepare for War Against Japan

Issued Important Declaration on the Current Situation

The Ten-Man Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps held a general meeting of members at the City Chamber of Commerce auditorium yesterday at 9:00 AM. Over a thousand members, including Zhu Maocheng, Mi Xingru, and Cai Jingzhen, attended. Zhu Maocheng, Mi Xingru, and Jiang Yingsheng were publicly elected as the presidium. The details of the various matters are recorded separately below:

The Chairman's Speech: Fellow members, at this critical moment of our nation's survival, everyone is enthusiastically and tragically gathering here with a spirit of great fearlessness, which is a manifestation of our national self-strengthening. (Omission) I hope that members will implement the tenets. Then China will definitely not be subjugated, and it will definitely not be a permanent semi-colony. Japanese imperialism will definitely not be able to invade at will, etc. Next, Cai Yuanpei, representing Ms. Cai Jingzhen, reported: My uncle expresses great sympathy for the Ten-Man Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps. He is very sorry that he cannot come today due to illness. Now that the country is in such dire straits, the people must have the determination to save themselves. At the same time, the tenets should be earnestly implemented, etc.

Important Resolutions: The proposal of the Ten-Man Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps' Liaison Organization Outline was passed. (1) The proposal to issue a declaration by the Corps was passed. (2) The proposal for all members to earnestly implement the third tenet and prepare for war against Japan was passed by public resolution as follows: (1) Frontline Work: A. Direct combat; B. Support (A) Rescuing wounded soldiers; (B) Rescuing victims; C. Propaganda; (A) Boosting morale; (B) Delivering news; (Methods) Item A: Each member will voluntarily join volunteer or formal troops. Items B and C: A battlefield service committee should be organized to plan and implement it. (2) Rear Area Work: A. Maintaining order: When military and police forces are deployed, they should be used to maintain order in the rear. (Methods) Promote the organization of defense or militia groups. B. Propaganda (A) Delivering war news; (B) Boosting morale; (C) Propagating various knowledge of defense and avoiding danger (Methods) (A) Organize lecture teams; (B) Edit publications and leaflets and slogans; Consoling families of battlefield workers; (Methods) Form a condolence team (3) Current Preparatory Work: A. Each member should join the volunteer army and receive military training. B. Invite military experts to lecture and guide on all common sense of military and defense matters, which will be planned and implemented by the Corps' Organizing Committee. C. Raise national salvation funds. During this national crisis, all members of the Corps must practice frugality, such as reducing entertainment consumption (tobacco, alcohol, cosmetics, etc.), banquets, clothing, weddings, funerals, etc., which can be saved at any time. Determine the amount to be saved each week according to each person's living situation, such as 10 cents or 1 yuan, and deposit it in a designated bank, which will be planned and implemented by the Corps' Organizing Committee. D. Recruit specialized talents to research and plan all the knowledge and plans needed for frontline and rear area work. (4) The proposal to expand the organization of the Ten-Man Corps was resolved and passed.

Declaration of the General Meeting: The declaration of the Ten-Man Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps' Hundred-Corps General Meeting stated: On September 18, 1931, Japanese imperialists took advantage of our tragic disasters and the fact that international powers were preoccupied with their own interests and had no time to look eastward, and suddenly used violence to first occupy Shenyang, seize Liaoning and Jilin, and invade our Heilongjiang, slaughtering our soldiers and civilians, plundering our wealth, destroying our cultural relics, undermining our sovereignty, disregarding justice, and abandoning humanity, not hesitating to open up unprecedented tragedies in order to achieve their conspiracy of aggression and annexation. We personally feel the pain and deeply resent it. Based on the responsibility of every citizen, we have contacted comrades and are implementing four simple tenets through the basic organization of ten people: (1) Do not buy Japanese goods; (2) Do not work for the Japanese; (3) Prepare for war against Japan; (4) Promote the organization of the Ten-Man Corps, trust each other, encourage each other, and strive to spread it throughout the country in the near future, gather the strength of 400 million people to defend ourselves and survive, so that justice may be extended and power may be eliminated. To this day, more than two months have passed. Our concessions have reached their limit, our patience has reached its limit, and the League of Nations is procrastinating and acting perfunctorily, disregarding the dignity of the covenant and its resolutions. Its struggling and pathetic state only serves to embolden the violent Japanese. As a result, our General Ma Zhanshan was forced to retreat north to Hailun, and alarming news from Jinzhou is frequently reported, and the sound of cannons in Tianjin has risen again. Moreover, the Japanese army is constantly increasing its reinforcements, and its ambition is becoming increasingly apparent. Its momentum will not stop until it destroys our country. We were born as Chinese and will die as Chinese ghosts. Our ancestors have passed down their legacy to us, and our descendants will continue it in the future. As long as there is a breath of life, we will never be willing to be reduced to prisoners. Seeing today's gathering of thousands of people, all with the determination to resist Japan and save the country, in the future, all our compatriots will unite in the same hatred and determination, and the day will not be far off. However, because the situation is critical, the entire country must be mobilized and move in unison in order to talk about saving the country. Therefore, there must be no more Qin-Yue states within the country, constantly at odds with each other, bickering over the rights, and pursuing disintegration. All grudges should be swept away at once. Even if we want to hold our heads and cry bitterly, and tell each other about our past mistakes, we will not have time for that. How much more so for those who are still scheming against each other and harming each other? If they still do not realize this, I really do not know what they are thinking. If they are still obsessed, they should admit that they have other intentions. Harmful horses must be removed, and traitors should be killed. We thousands of people swear to abandon them together with the people of the country. The situation is urgent. Three million square miles of territory are being trampled under the iron hooves of the violent Japanese, and thirty million compatriots are being bombarded by the violent Japanese cannons. Smoke and fire obscure our vision, and the sound of war drums frightens our hearts. We thousands of people swear to exhaust our blood and sincerity, and are willing to join the people of the country to resist the violent Japanese in order to save the country. If we slack off or disobey, may heaven and earth punish us. This declaration is made with utmost sincerity.

Tax Police Battalion Commander Xie Mingdan 116

Fell from a Horse and Was Crushed to Death

The Corpse Was Crushed into Three Sections, and the Skull Was Shattered

Brain Matter and Fresh Blood Flowed Together, a Tragic Sight

Xie Mingdan, the battalion commander of the Second Battalion of the First Regiment of the Special Service Corps of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government's Tax Police, was transferred back to Wusong from Nantong the night before. Currently, because the empty houses in Songzhen are all occupied by the troops of the 19th Route Army, the troops of the battalion had no place to live. Therefore, yesterday, the troops were transferred to Jiangwan to be stationed. After the troops set off, Battalion Commander Xie rode his horse with several guards, heading south along the railway from the Yuncaobang Bridge, and when he reached the factory entrance of the railway general machine gate north of Zhanghuabang, a local villager was walking in the railway track ahead. Battalion Commander Xie, with good intentions, immediately beckoned the villager to jump out of the railway. When he was about to urge his horse to start walking, the horse's foot accidentally got stuck in the track and could not move. However, the train had already arrived, and the driver, due to the rapid speed, was unable to brake in time, causing the front of the train to hit the horse's buttocks. The horse jumped around in pain, and Battalion Commander Xie fell into the track and was crushed by the wheels in the crook of his leg, cut into three sections. Both legs were separated from the body, and the skull was also crushed, a bloody and blurred scene that was too horrible to bear. The corpse was dragged by the wheels to the factory gate about two to three feet away to the south. The snow-white brain matter and bright red fresh blood were stuck to the railway track and sleepers where the corpse stopped, which was very regrettable. After the accident, the battalion's secretary, Tang, immediately reported to the regiment headquarters. The corpse has not yet been collected. It is said that it will be collected after the regiment commander arrives for inspection. People have been ordered to build a cool shed and send troops to guard it. The horse was also seriously injured. When Xie's subordinates heard the news and rushed to the scene, they cried incessantly. It is reported that Battalion Commander Xie was 32 years old, from Anyue County, Sichuan Province. After graduating from Tsinghua University in Beiping, he stayed at the University of Virginia in the United States. After returning to China, he took his current position. He married last year, and his family is still in Sichuan. He has a younger brother who is currently studying at Tsinghua University in Beiping. He has no relatives in Shanghai, and his afterlife is very miserable.

Son-in-law Wins Inheritance Lawsuit for Grandchildren 117

Grandchildren Inherit Maternal Grandfather's Estate

First Case of Its Kind in Shanghai

Subrogation Inheritance Not Without Reason

Request for Provisional Execution Rejected

Qin Fang, daughter of wealthy merchant Xue Baorun and former wife of Hua Lihou, passed away after giving birth to two children. Last year, Xue Baorun passed away, and his family became involved in lawsuits over the distribution of his estate. Hua, believing that his deceased wife Qin Fang also had the right to inherit part of the estate, hired lawyers Yang Linzhi, Qi Shaoying, and Zhang Jiahui to represent his children, Hua Yigu and Hua Manyun, in a lawsuit against Xue Baorun's sons, Yan Sheng, Jia Sheng, Gen Sheng, and Gan Sheng, in the First Special District Court, seeking a share of the estate. Because both plaintiffs were minors, Hua Lihou appeared in court as their legal guardian to make statements. The defendants hired lawyers Lin Yingqing and Wang Youling to defend them. After several court hearings, the court ruled in favor of the plaintiffs, allowing the grandchildren to inherit their maternal grandfather's estate, the first case of its kind in the city. The defendants, dissatisfied with the verdict, intend to appeal to the High Court. The first instance judgment is appended below:

(Main Text) The defendants shall pay the plaintiffs two-thirds of the 500,000 yuan inheritance share that the deceased Hua Xueqin Fang was entitled to. The remaining claims of the plaintiffs and their request for provisional execution are rejected. The plaintiffs shall bear one-third of the litigation costs, and the defendants shall bear two-thirds. (Facts) The plaintiffs' representatives stated that the defendants should be ordered to pay 500,000 yuan. Their statement briefly stated: Xue Baorun, the plaintiffs' maternal grandfather, had seven children: four sons, the defendants Xue Gansheng, Yan Sheng, Jia Sheng, and Gen Sheng, and three daughters, Hua Xueqin Fang, Xu Xuechaoqun, and Xue Baobao. Hua Xueqin Fang, the plaintiffs' mother, gave birth to the plaintiffs and Hua Yiheng. Unfortunately, she passed away on February 20th of the Republic of China year eight. The maternal grandfather, Xue Baorun, also passed away recently, on August 25th of the Republic of China year nineteen, leaving behind approximately 2 million yuan in assets, all of which are managed by the defendants. Except for Xue Bao's inheritance share, which has already been resolved separately, the share that the plaintiffs' mother should inherit, calculated at one-sixth, should be 500,000 yuan. According to the Judicial Yuan's Interpretations Nos. 405 and 424 of the Republic of China year twenty, the plaintiffs should inherit by subrogation. Whether a woman has the right to inherit property should be determined at the time the inheritance begins. The date of the woman's death is irrelevant. The defendants are still jointly managing the aforementioned estate and have not divided it, which does not involve the provisions of Article 3 of the Implementation Law of the Inheritance Compilation. A person inheriting by subrogation can claim the entire inheritance share of the person being subrogated. It is permissible for the plaintiffs' brother, Hua Yiheng, not to be included among the plaintiffs. Furthermore, the defendants are currently extravagant. Xue Baorun has only been dead for a year, and the defendants have already spent a considerable amount of the estate. In the future, they may not be able to repay their debts. Therefore, they request a declaration of provisional execution. The defendants' representatives responded, stating that it is true that one-sixth of Xue Baorun's estate should be 500,000 yuan. However, the plaintiffs' mother died in the Republic of China year eight. At that time, women did not have the right to inherit property. The right to inherit property cannot be retroactively applied to the plaintiffs' mother simply because women had the right to inherit property when Xue Baorun died. The plaintiffs fundamentally have no basis for subrogation inheritance. Furthermore, the defendants had already divided Xue Baorun's estate and had an estate management certificate issued by the court. According to the provisions of Article 2 of the Implementation Law of the Inheritance Compilation, there is no room for the defendants to inherit by subrogation. Furthermore, of the plaintiffs' three siblings, Hua Yiheng was not included as a plaintiff, and it is inappropriate for the plaintiffs to claim the entire inheritance share of their mother. As for the defendants' sale of part of the industry, it was used to repay Xue Baorun's debts. There are still 3 million yuan in assets, and it is highly unlikely that they would not be able to pay 500,000 yuan. The plaintiffs' request for provisional execution is clearly inconsistent with the law. They submitted a photograph of the estate management certificate as evidence. (Reason) The defendants' representatives admitted that one-sixth of Xue Baorun's estate should be 500,000 yuan. The issues to be examined are (1) Whether the plaintiffs can claim subrogation inheritance because their mother died in the Republic of China year eight; (2) Whether the defendants had divided Xue Baorun's property; (3) Whether the plaintiffs can claim the entire inheritance share of their mother; (4) Whether provisional execution should be declared. Regarding the first point, whether a woman has the right to inherit property should be determined at the time the inheritance begins, i.e., when the deceased dies, and not when the woman dies. If a woman had the right to inherit property at the time of her death, but the woman no longer had the right to inherit property when the deceased died, then her direct descendants would have no room for subrogation inheritance. Conversely, if a woman did not have the right to inherit property at the time of her death, but women had the right to inherit property when the deceased died, then her direct descendants could claim subrogation inheritance. In this case, although the plaintiffs' mother did not have the right to inherit property at the time of her death, women had the right to inherit property when Xue Baorun died. The plaintiffs' claim for subrogation inheritance is not without reason. Regarding the second point, the defendants argued that Xue Baorun's estate had been divided, relying on the estate management certificate issued by this court. However, the certificate stated that the defendants were jointly managing the estate and did not mention any division. The defendants' argument is clearly untenable. Regarding the third point, the plaintiffs are claiming the right to inherit by subrogation themselves, which is different from claiming the right to inherit on behalf of their mother. They can only sue for the share they are entitled to inherit by subrogation and should not include the share that other persons inheriting by subrogation are entitled to inherit. The defendants' argument on this point should be considered reasonable. Regarding the fourth point, the defendants are managing an estate of 3 million yuan, which the plaintiffs' representatives do not dispute. The plaintiffs are only requesting 500,000 yuan, so it is highly unlikely that they will not be able to afford it in the future. Their request for a declaration of provisional execution is inconsistent with the provisions of Article 463, Paragraph 1, of the Civil Procedure Law and cannot be approved. Based on the above conclusions and in accordance with Article 98 of the Civil Procedure Law, the judgment is made as in the main text. November 3rd of the Republic of China year twenty, Judge Li Moyin of the Civil Division of the First Special District Court of Jiangsu, Shanghai.
