Youth Corner

Awakening 169

— Cheng

The continuous drizzle has made our joyful mood, following the gloomy weather, also become gloomy. In the classroom, several classmates, full of energy, blew out the melody of the famous movie song "Ramona" from their harmonicas. But although the sound of the harmonica was still as clear and melodious as before, and as pleasing to our ears, the singing of the classmates to the sound of the harmonica was not as happy, not as melodious, and not as foot-tapping as before, as if they were about to prepare to dance. Really, how can an unhappy mood be made happy, except for that true and automatic happiness?

"Oh, this stuffy weather, stuffy rain, stuffy classroom, stuffy homework, it's really suffocating us to death!" Yang said after the sound of the harmonica stopped, with a "stuffy" character in each sentence.

"Originally, being a student is of course stuffy. Aren't we even more stuffy than birds trapped in cages? Although birds are trapped in their narrow world, their cries, their jumps, their eats are all free. When they feel happy, they freely cry or jump. When they want to eat, they eat some food. There is nothing uncomfortable. But we are not as free as birds trapped in cages. The 'dang...' of the class bell fundamentally stops our liveliness, our wanting to do whatever we want to do, our wanting to say whatever we want to say!" Classmate Wang complained. She loves freedom the most. She thinks all the rules in the school seem to bind her rigidly.

"To be honest, school is a place that eats people. If my dad didn't force me to go to school, I would definitely not be sitting stuffily in the classroom like this. Think about it, what we learn is not what we will use in society in the future. So we are wasting our energy to diligently research it." Wang's comrade Lu continued. She is very smart, but usually she doesn't do in-depth research on anything, like homework. She is a negative person who holds the sixty-point doctrine. After the exam, she got the news that she "might pass," and she was so happy about it.

We all regret Wang and Lu, for using their agile brains to work on writing love letters. They despise being at the top of the list, and do not require scores above sixty points. Therefore, the two of them are willing to fall behind silently, and are unwilling to compete with anyone, nor are they jealous of anyone. Therefore, the words "friends of sloppy mud" have become their nicknames.

"It is indeed a waste of energy to diligently research it. Think about it, how easy it is to be a Lady. What we are currently learning, which Lady has ever used it? What Ladies need to know is just how to serve their husbands." Shen said dimly, seeming to sigh. She absolutely regretted Wang and Lu, so the more she regretted, the more she used words to ridicule them. At the same time, Shen is such a person, advocating that in school, one subject must be mastered. Several classmates have ridiculed her, and she said frankly, "Since it is not necessary to know everything completely, why does the school have to require us to read everything, and to pass?" We couldn't think of appropriate words to answer her, so we just shouted "Good student, good student."

Shen's sarcastic words did not have any repercussions for Wang and Lu. They said indifferently, as if they didn't care, "Say whatever you want, say whatever you want."

We were also silent, not adding any opinions to either side.

○　　　　○　　　　　○

Today in Chinese class, the teacher returned our composition books. After everyone took them from the teacher's hand, they all lowered their heads to read. Only Wang and Lu were still sitting uneasily, looking up at the teacher.

"Wang and Lu definitely won't pass," a voice gently entered my ear.

But the teacher suddenly said aloud with a smile, "Wang ×× and Lu ××, this time their compositions have improved a lot. The meaning of their writing is better than anyone else's. I will explain it to you... ... ... ... ... ... ... ... ... ... "

While we were quietly listening, we were thinking that they probably had an awakening after listening to Shen's words.

Different Teachers 170

— Jin

The English teacher hurried into the classroom, panting and wiping the sweat from his forehead. His two bony eyes looked around nervously, and that situation really made people pity him.

"Oh, teacher, so early. Class has been in session for ten minutes!" Ms. Zhang said to the teacher with a mocking expression.

"Oh, class has been in session for ten minutes? No, it seems early," the teacher said in surprise while looking at his watch.

"Then why not sit and rest at home for a while longer?" Ms. Zhang said coldly.

"Ha, teacher, your watch is probably sleeping," Ling said to the teacher with a cheerful smile.

"Oh, yes, my watch is slow," the teacher said slowly.

"So your watch is slow. But when it's time for class, the bell won't ring because you haven't come. It's unlikely that it will ring when you come," Ms. Zhang said to the teacher hatefully, revealing a contemptuous expression.

"Teacher, call the roll," Ling seemed a little impatient with Ms. Zhang's words. She glared at Ms. Zhang hatefully, and then said to the teacher.

The teacher slowly put down the roll call book and called the roll. His expression was helpless.

While calling the roll, Ling said softly to her seatmate Juan, "There's no such thing. The teacher was a few minutes late, and she's so rude to the teacher. Really, the teacher is too kind... Hey, look, she's making faces at the teacher."

Hearing this, I couldn't help but quickly turn my head to look at her. I saw Ms. Zhang closing her eyes, opening her mouth wide, and shaking her tongue rapidly from left to right.

At this time, the teacher was teaching, and it was very quiet.

"I don't understand, I don't understand, I don't understand what you're saying!" Ms. Zhang immediately broke the silence, shouting like a riot, and didn't listen to the teacher repeating the section for her. She just chatted and laughed with her classmates sitting in a corner.

"Hey, look at the teacher's robe. It's so big and long, haha, isn't he like a big lantern?" Zhen began to criticize the teacher.

"No, he looks more like a clown on the stage," Fen followed her.

"I hate his face the most. It looks like a crying ghost. That mouth moves and moves like an old woman. And those hairs don't comb it light, you don't see like a rotten rice stalk?"

"I hate his annoying voice the most. It's not like Mandarin, it's not like dialect. Listening to it makes people want to throw up even rice. Listen, "ze gou" "ze gou" I don't know why he has to read it like that. Can't he read "this"?" Rui said softly.

"Oh, how come, teacher, you're talking so fast?" Ms. Zhang said with a surprised look.

"It's not fast, maybe you're not listening," the teacher said.

"How do you know I'm not listening? I was clearly listening," Ms. Zhang said angrily.

"Then I'll ask you, where did I talk to?" the teacher said.

"Why do you ask me when you're lecturing? Did you forget where you talked to?" Ms. Zhang said with a red face.

Dang, dang, dang, finally the class was over. The teacher hurriedly ran out of the classroom, as if escaping from hell.

○　　　○　　　○

The next one was political science. Class had been in session for a long time, but the teacher hadn't come yet, so the students started rioting. Suddenly, a series of crisp leather shoe sounds knocked in the corridor. After a while, the classroom door opened. The political science teacher was wearing a brand new suit, with a felt hat on his head, and carrying a large black leather bag in his hand. His shoulders were raised up, as if carrying a load on a pole, and he walked in.

Ms. Zhang started talking to the teacher again, "Oh, teacher, why are you late today? We've been waiting for a long time, almost a quarter of an hour!"

"Oh, no, it's still early," the teacher said slowly, looking at Ms. Zhang.

"Yes, it's still early, I'm afraid class hasn't even started yet... the time to dismiss class is coming soon."

"Oh, don't bother so much. What's the point of rioting like this?" Ms. Zhang suddenly broke their conversation and said seriously.

This class was really quiet, no one was rioting. Ms. Zhang quietly looked at the teacher's glowing hair, with a smile on her face. In the silence, the sound of Ms. Zhang's conversation in that corner could be heard.

"The teacher's hair is really shiny. I wonder what he put on it. It's also a little fragrant. Can you smell it?" Ms. Zhang said, staring blankly at the teacher's face.

"I can't smell it. Your sense of smell can be considered extremely sensitive," Hui said coldly.

"His suit is really good-looking. Comparing it with the English teacher's robe, it's really a world apart," Ms. Zhang said again.

"Hey, Zhang, you're a little... you probably love him," Hui said to Zhang jokingly.

"Bah, don't talk nonsense," Ms. Zhang said with a red face.

"Hey, Zhang, his face is really beautiful, look, why don't you look?" Yun said to Zhang with a smile.

"Oh, his hair is really fragrant, shiny and bright, it can reflect your face from his hair, but it's your mirror of love," Juan said in the silence, revealing a contemptuous expression, ridiculing.

To Literary Youth 171

— Qiu

Turning every tear into a bullet,

I wish every writer would become a warrior,

Throwing down the pen that sings of wind and moon,

Raise the sharp gun and stab the dwarf slaves with all our might,

Raise the sharp gun and stab the dwarf slaves with all our might,

Do not worry about your own life and death,

Shake your spirits and courageous courage,

No blood can wash away the great shame of the country,

No blood can wash away the great shame of the country,

No blood can erect the banner of victory,

Valuable bloodshed is glorious and great,

It will create the history of national survival,

You see, the dwarf slaves are coming to your side like tigers and wolves,

Don't sing about the wind and moon, holding your heart in love,

Don't dream in the ivory palace anymore,

Don't wander in the crossroads anymore, wander,

You hear, the gunfire of the dwarf slaves is approaching step by step,

If you are not deaf, you should not groan without illness anymore

Wake up, let's unite and fight the dwarf slaves desperately,

Any later, we will have no life to fight,
